        console.log('asd');
       function SetCookie(name,value){
            var Days = 30; //此 cookie 将被保存 30 days
            var exp = new Date();    //new Date("December 31, 9998");
            exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + Days*24*60*60*1000);
            document.cookie = name + "="+ escape (value) + ";expires=" + exp.toGMTString()+";path=/; domain=.360eol.com";
        }
    function getCookie(name){
        var arr = document.cookie.match(new RegExp("(^| )"+name+"=([^;]*)(;|$)"));
        if(arr != null) return unescape(arr[2]); return null;
    }
       
    // 分站管理
$(function() {
     var province_mark = getCookie('province_mark');
    if (province_mark != 'true') {
         var province= getCookie('province');
        if (province != null && province.length > 0 && province != 'undefined' && province != 'www') {
            location.href = 'http://' + province + '.360eol.com/';
        } else {
            var state = remote_ip_info.province; //获取省份
            var arr = {
                "江苏": "jiangsu","安徽": "anhui","浙江": "zhejiang","山东": "shandong","上海": "shanghai","北京": "beijing","陕西": "shanxi","江西": "jiangxi","河南": "henan","湖南": "hunan","重庆": "chongqing"
            };
            if (arr[state]) {
               location.href = 'http://' + arr[state] + '.360eol.com/';
                SetCookie('province', arr[state]);
            }else{
                $('body').show(); 
            }
        }
    }else{
        SetCookie('province_mark ','false');
        $('body').show(); 
    }
    
      $('#top_navcity').on('click', 'a', function(event) {
        SetCookie('province',$(this).attr('class'));
      });
    
    });
    </script>

function newgetCookie(name){ 
 var cookie_start = document.cookie.indexOf(name);
 var cookie_end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", cookie_start);
 return cookie_start == -1 ? '' : document.cookie.substring(cookie_start + name.length + 1,cookie_end );
}

                    <script type="text/javascript">
                    function submitsearch(){
                        $("#head_search").submit();
                }
                $(function() {
                $('.show-wx').hover(function() {
                    $('.top-wx').toggle();
                });
                $('.btn').on('click', function(event) {
                	event.preventDefault();
                	if ($('.search').find('span').text()=='新闻') {
                		submitsearch();
                	} else{
                		window.open('http://school.360eol.com/Home/Index/index/school_name/'+$('.search-text').val());
                	}
                });
$('.search-text').on('focus', function(event) {
    $(document).on('keydown', function(event) {
        if (event.keyCode == 13) {
            if ($('.search').find('span').text() == '新闻') {
                submitsearch();
            } else {
                window.open('http://school.360eol.com/Home/Index/index/school_name/' + $('.search-text').val());
            }
        }
    });
});
            });
	</script>

                <script type="text/javascript">
                // 热门高校
                jQuery(function() {
                    // 初始化
                    var area = [];
                    schoolGZ(0, area[0], '高招院校', 0);
                    schoolGZ(0, area[0], '研招院校', 1);
                    schoolGZ(0, area[0], '高职高专', 2);
                    $('#myTab0 li').each(function(index, el) {
                        if (index == 0) {
                            area[index] = $(this).find('span').text();
                        } else {
                            area[index] = $(this).find('span').text() + '省';
                        }
                    });
                    $('#myTab0').on('mouseover', 'li', function(event) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        var num = $(this).attr('data-class');
                        schoolGZ(num, area[num], '高招院校', 0);
                        schoolGZ(num, area[num], '研招院校', 1);
                        schoolGZ(num, area[num], '高职高专', 2);
                    });
                    // console.log(area);


                    function schoolGZ(num, address, schooltype, type) {
                            if (address == "热门学校") {
                                address = null;
                            }
                            $.ajax({
                                    url: 'http://school.360eol.com/CommentApi/school_index',
                                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                                    data: {
                                        num: 24,
                                        address: address,
                                        schooltype: schooltype,
                                    },
                                })
                                .done(function(data) {
                                    //console.log(data);
                                    if (data != null) {
                                        var html = "";
                                        $.each(data, function(index, val) {
                                            html += '<li><div><a target="_blank" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html" class="bluelink">' + val.school_name + '</a></div><div><a target="_blank" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html" class="greylink">口碑</a><a target="_blank" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html" class="greylink">图库</a></div></li>';
                                        });
                                        
                                        if ($('#myTab0_Content' + num).find('.type' + type).html()=='') {
                                            // console.log(html);
                                        $('#myTab0_Content' + num).find('.type' + type).html(html);
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                        }
                        // 点击
                    var i = 8;
                    jQuery(document).on('click', '.right-click', function(event) {
                        var page = jQuery(this).attr('data-id');
                        var v_show = jQuery(this).parent().prev("dd").find('.hot-length');
                        var v_width = v_show.find('li').width() * 8;
                        var len = v_show.find('li').length;
                        var page_count = Math.ceil(len / i);
                        if (!v_show.is(":animated")) {
                            if (page == page_count) { //最后一页点击返回到第一页
                                v_show.animate({
                                    left: '0px'
                                }, "slow");
                                page = 1;
                                jQuery(this).attr('data-id', 1);
                            } else {
                                v_show.animate({
                                    left: '-=' + v_width
                                }, "slow");
                                jQuery(this).attr('data-id', ++page);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                    jQuery(document).on('click', '.left-click', function(event) {
                        var page = jQuery(this).closest('.hotcar-list').find('.right-click').attr('data-id');
                        //console.log('上一页1' + page);
                        var v_show = jQuery(this).parent().next().find('.hot-length');
                        var v_width = v_show.find('li').width() * 8;
                        if (!v_show.is(":animated")) {
                            if (v_show.css("left") != "0px") {
                                v_show.animate({
                                    left: '+=' + v_width
                                }, "slow");
                                jQuery(this).closest('.hotcar-list').find('.right-click').attr('data-id', --page);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                       

                    

                });
                </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
        $('.eol').on('click', '.function01-sortmore', function(event) {
            window.open("http://school.360eol.com/");

        });
        var school_province = '';
        var school_run = '';
        var school_feature = '';
        sessionStorage.setItem('school_type', 1);
        $('#myTab1').on('mouseover', 'a', function(event) {
            var num = parseInt($(this).attr('data-id'));
            sessionStorage.setItem('school_type', num);

        });


        $('.school-province').on('click', 'a', function(event) {
            school_province = '/prs/' + $(this).text();
            var text=$(this).text();
            $('.school-province').each(function(index, el) {
            	$(this).prev().find('span').html(text);
            });
            console.log(school_province);
        });
        $('.school-run').on('click', 'a', function(event) {
            school_run = '/prs2/' + $(this).text();
            var text=$(this).text();
            $('.school-run').each(function(index, el) {
            	$(this).prev().find('span').html(text);
            });
        });
        $('.school-feature').on('click', 'a', function(event) {
            school_feature = '/prs5/' + $(this).text();
            var text=$(this).text();
            $('.school-feature').each(function(index, el) {
            	$(this).prev().find('span').html(text);
            });
        });
        $('.tab-content').on('click', 'a.btn-blue', function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            var school_type = sessionStorage.getItem('school_type');
            var search_url = 'http://school.360eol.com/CommentApi/index_select/school_type/' + school_type + school_province + school_run + school_feature;
            //console.log(search_url);
            window.open(search_url);
        });
        $('.car-select').on('click', '.select', function(event) {
            $(this).find('.select-option').show().closest('.select').siblings().find('.select-option').hide();
        });
        hotSchool('高招院校', 'gzyx');
        hotSchool('研究生院', 'yjsy');
        hotSchool('高职高专', 'dlxx');

        function hotSchool(schooltype, class_) {
            $.ajax({
                    url: 'http://school.360eol.com/CommentApi/school_index',
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    data: {
                        schooltype: schooltype,
                        num: 5
                    },
                })
                .done(function(data) {
                    //  console.log(data);
                    var html = "";
                    $.each(data, function(index, val) {
                        if (index == 0) {
                            html = '热门学校：<a target="_blank" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html">' + val.school_name + '</a>';
                        } else {
                            html += '|<a target="_blank" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html">' + val.school_name + '</a>';
                        }
                    });
                    $('.' + class_).before(html);
                });
        }
        </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function() {
        	goodColleges('',0);
        	$('#myTab4').on('mousemove', 'li', function(event) {
        		event.preventDefault();
        		var num=$('#myTab4 li').index(this);
        		// alert(num);
        		var province=$(this).find('span').text()+'省';
        		if (province=="热门省") {
        			province="";
        		}
        		goodColleges(province,num);
        	});
        });
		function goodColleges(site,num){
			$.ajax({
                    url: 'http://school.360eol.com/CommentApi/school_comment',
                    // dataType: 'default: Intelligent Guess (Other values: xml, json, script, or html)',
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    data: {
                        address: site,
                    },
                })
                .done(function(data) {
                    // console.log("success");
                    // console.log(data);
                    var html = '<dl class="market-list"><dt><div class="market-text01">校名</div><div class="market-text02">口碑</div><div class="market-text03">评价</div></dt>';
                    // var comment=0;
                    $.each(data, function(index, val) {
                    	if (val.comment==null) {
                    		val.comment=0;
                    	}
                        if (index != 0 && index != 27 && (index + 1) % 7 == 1) {
                            html += ' </dl><div class="market-border"></div><dl class="market-list"><dt><div class="market-text01">校名</div><div class="market-text02">口碑</div><div class="market-text03">评价</div></dt>';
                        }
                        html += '<dd><div class="market-text01"><a target="_blank" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html">' + val.school_name + '</a></div><div class="market-text02"><a target="_blank" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html">' + val.school_ratings + '分</a></div><div class="market-text03"><a target="_blank" class="red" href="http://school.360eol.com/School/index/school_id/' + val.school_id + '.html">' + val.comment + '次</a></div></dd>';
                        if (index == 27) {
                            html += '</dl>';
                        }
                    });
                    // console.log(html);
                    if ($('#myTab4_Content'+num).html()=="") {
                    	$('#myTab4_Content'+num).html(html);
                    }
                })
                .fail(function() {
                   // console.log("error");
                })
                .always(function() {
                  // console.log("complete");
                });
		}
        </script>
